# V2ME Dismantlement V1.0.0 by Bob Bobington & Dr, Configured as a basis for implimentation in new mods.

# ID Groups:
#	0400-0409				Configuration & Trigger Events 
#	0410-0419				First Wave Bounce Events (Ai)
#	0420-0429 & 0800-0899 	Dismantlement Leader Decision Events
#	0430-0439				Second Wave Bounce Events (Ai)
#	0440-0449				Primary Effect Bouncing Events
#	0450-0479				Primary Victor Response Events
#	0480-0489				Secondary First Wave Bounce Events (Ai)
#	0490-0499				Secondary Victor Leading Decision Events
#	0500-0509				Secondary Second Wave Bounce Events (Ai)
#	0510-0519				Secondary Effect Bouncing Evenets
#	0520-0549				Secondary Victor Response Events
#	0550-0559				Effect Events
#	1100-1199 & 1200-1299	Custom Formables Bounce Events & Puppet Custom Formables Bounce Events
#	1300-1399 & 1400-1499	Custom Formables Decision Events & Puppet Formables Decision Events
#

##### 0400-0409	Configuration & Trigger Events #####

country_event = {
    id = 777770403
    title = "The $CAPITAL$ Conference has been called!"
    desc = "This decision is to inform you the following events will allow you to dismantle recent enemies."
	picture = "Dismantle 2"
	major = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#sets defeated value for newly defeated countries
		
		set_global_flag = waiting_for_dismantlement_setup
		
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = Major_Defeated
			}
			clr_country_flag = Major_Defeated
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 1.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 1 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 1.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 2.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 2 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 2.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 3.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 3 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 3.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 4.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 4 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 4.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 5.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 5 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 5.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 6.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 6 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 6.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 7.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 7 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 7.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 8.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 8 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				alliance_with = THIS
				is_greater_power = yes
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = potential_conference_member value = 0.99 }
					check_variable = { which = potential_conference_member_overflow value = 0.99 }
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						check_variable = { which = potential_conference_member value = 0.99 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = potential_conference_member value = 1.99 } }
						THIS = {
							check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0.99 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 1.99 } }
						}
						NOT = {
							war_countries = {
								check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0.99 }
								NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 1.99 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				owner = {
					set_variable = { which = part_of_conference value = 1 }
					set_variable = { which = potential_conference_member value = 0 }
				}
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						check_variable = { which = potential_conference_member_overflow value = 0.99 }
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = potential_conference_member_overflow value = 1.99 } }
						THIS = {
							check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0.99 }
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 1.99 } }

#
					}
					civilized = no
				}
			}

		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }

						}
					}
				}

				exists = yes
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Core_Event_Sent value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }
			}
			set_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Rewritable_State value = 0 }
		}

		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_vassal = yes
					is_substate = yes
				}
				overlord = {
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}

#staggers the dismantlement events so they don't all spam out at once
country_event = {
	id = 777770408
	title = "AI: Dismantlement Event Trigger"
	desc = "AI: Dismantlement Event Trigger"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Trigger Events"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = mail_delivery_opened
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 0.99 } }
			}
			THIS = { clr_country_flag = mail_delivery_ready_for_pickup set_country_flag = clear_secondaries set_country_flag = clear_modifiers }
			clr_country_flag = mail_delivery_opened
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = clear_modifiers } }
			owner = {
				any_country = {
					clr_country_flag = common_government_bonus
					clr_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty
					clr_country_flag = infamous_penalty
					clr_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty
					clr_country_flag = recent_state_bonus
					clr_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus
					clr_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty
				}
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = clear_secondaries } }
			owner = {
				clr_country_flag = clear_secondaries
				any_country = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { which = Secondary_Claim value = 0.99 }
					}
					set_variable = { which = Secondary_Claim value = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = too_many_deliveries
#
#		existing cores
#
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { THIS = { has_country_flag = mail_delivery_ready_for_pickup } }
				any_core = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
							overlord = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = part_of_conference value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { overlord = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } } }
				exists = yes
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Core_Event_Sent value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }
				check_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 0.99 }
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = colonial_zone_exclusion
				}
			}
			country_event = 777770412
			set_country_flag = mail_delivery_opened
			set_variable = { which = Core_Event_Sent value = 1 }
			CLN = { set_country_flag = mail_delivery_ready_for_pickup }
		}

#		puppet union events

#		EXAMPLE MERGER PUPPET EVENT
#
#		Note! If a country has two different possible dismantlement unions and requires a custom menu it will also need an event here.
#
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { THIS = { has_country_flag = mail_delivery_ready_for_pickup } }
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_vassal = yes
					is_substate = yes
				}
				OR = {
#					tag = EXAMPLE_TAG
#					tag = EXAMPLE_TAG
#					tag = EXAMPLE_TAG
#					tag = EXAMPLE_TAG
				}
				overlord = {
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = part_of_conference value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Puppet_Event_Sent value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }
				check_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 0.99 }
			}
			country_event = 777771200
			set_country_flag = mail_delivery_opened
			set_variable = { which = Puppet_Event_Sent value = 1 }
			CLN = { set_country_flag = mail_delivery_ready_for_pickup }
		}
		
#
#		Base Event for puppets - MUST COME AFTER PUPPET UNION EVENTS
#
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { THIS = { has_country_flag = mail_delivery_ready_for_pickup } }
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					is_vassal = yes
					is_substate = yes
				}
				overlord = {
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = part_of_conference value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Puppet_Event_Sent value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }

##### 0410-0419	First Wave Bounce Events (Ai) #####


country_event = {
    id = 777770410
	#no pic needed
    title = "Is this what freedom feels like?"
    desc = "Our freedom is being considered."
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = core_count value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = pop_count value = 0 }
		all_core = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
			}
			THIS = { change_variable = { which = core_count value = 1 } }
		}
		all_core = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				THIS = { change_variable = { which = pop_count value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
    option = {
        name = "Very Well"
		set_variable = { which = Rewritable_State value = 1 }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = too_many_deliveries } }
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = Total_One_Victor }
				OR = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 2.99 } }
				THIS = { OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 20 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 150 } } } }
			}
			FROM = { set_country_flag = too_many_deliveries }
			THIS = { set_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 1 } }
			country_event = 777770802
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = too_many_deliveries } }
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = Total_One_Victor }
				OR = { AND = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 2.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 5.99 } } }
				THIS = { AND = { NOT = { OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 20 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 150 } } } OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 15 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 100 } } } } }
			}
			FROM = { set_country_flag = too_many_deliveries }
			THIS = { set_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 1 } }
			country_event = 777770426
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = too_many_deliveries } }
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = Total_One_Victor }
				check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 5.99 }
				THIS = { NOT = { OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 15 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 100 } } } }
			}
			FROM = { set_country_flag = too_many_deliveries }
			THIS = { set_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 1 } }
			country_event = 777770420
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = too_many_deliveries } }
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
				has_global_flag = Total_One_Victor
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 2.99 } }
				THIS = { OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 20 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 150 } } } }
			}
			FROM = { set_country_flag = too_many_deliveries }
			THIS = { set_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 1 } }
			country_event = 777770805
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = too_many_deliveries } }
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
				has_global_flag = Total_One_Victor
				AND = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 2.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 5.99 } } }
				THIS = { AND = { NOT = { OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 20 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 150 } } } OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 15 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 100 } } } } }
			}
			FROM = { set_country_flag = too_many_deliveries }
			THIS = { set_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 1 } }
			country_event = 777770429
		}

country_event = {
    id = 777770411
    title = "We may be give independence from $FROMCOUNTRY$ by the current dismantlement!"
    desc = "Our puppethood by $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ is under review."
	picture = "Dismantle 4"
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {

		set_variable = { which = pop_count value = 0 }

					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
			}
			THIS = { change_variable = { which = core_count value = 1 } }
		}

			}

			}
		}
	}
	
    option = {

				NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 2.99 } }
			}

		}
		any_country = {

country_event = {
    id = 777770420
    title = "What would you like to do with $FROMCOUNTRY$?"
    desc = "The concept of $FROMCOUNTRY$ is present within the borders of the defeated, should we demand the creation of a $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ state?"
	picture = "Dismantle 3"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
#	Set Probability Variables	
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			which = dismantlement_dollars
			value = 15
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				have_core_in = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_recently_lost_war = yes
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }
	
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall exist (Overwrite new states)"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_Overwrite value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770430
		}
		create_alliance = FROM
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 5 government = democracy }
			modifier = { factor = 5 relation = { who = FROM value = 199 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 relation = { who = FROM value = 180 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 relation = { who = FROM value = 160 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 140 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			 
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall exist"

country_event = {

	picture = "Dismantle 3"

    is_triggered_only = yes

		set_variable = {
			which = dismantlement_dollars
			value = 15
		}

			limit = {

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}

				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }

			}

	allow_multiple_instances = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {

				tag = FROM
				have_core_in = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_recently_lost_war = yes
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}

				tag = FROM

				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }

			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }

				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }

        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall exist (Overwrite new states)"

            factor = 3
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = common_government_bonus }

			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }

    }

country_event = {
    id = 777770803
    title = "What should be done with the $FROMCOUNTRY$ puppet state?"
    desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ is a puppet regime, should we reorganize their government?"
	picture = "Dismantle 1"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
#	Set Probability Variables	
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				have_core_in = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_recently_lost_war = yes
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }
	
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall be independent!"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Puppet_Freedom value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770431
		}
		create_alliance = FROM
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 5 government = democracy }
			modifier = { factor = 5 relation = { who = FROM value = 199 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 relation = { who = FROM value = 180 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 relation = { who = FROM value = 160 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 140 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			 
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "We do not care about $FROMCOUNTRY$"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Puppet_Apathy value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770431
		}
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 1 has_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 1 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall remain as it is"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Puppet_As_Is value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 0 }
			country_event = 777770431
		}
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 1
			modifier = { factor = 1 has_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 5 has_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 1 badboy = 17 }
        }

    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				have_core_in = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_recently_lost_war = yes
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }

		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite

				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				have_core_in = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_recently_lost_war = yes
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite

				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Eighth_Victor_Complete value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770432
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = Seventh_Victor_Complete value = 0.99 } } check_variable = { which = Sixth_Victor_Complete value = 0.99 } }
				tag = FROM
			}
			set_variable = { which = Seventh_Victor_Complete value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770432
		}
		any_country = {

##### 0480-0489	Secondary First Wave Bounce Events (Ai) #####


country_event = {
    id = 777770480
    title = "Is this what freedom feels like?"
    desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ is deciding our fate."
	picture = "dismantle 1"
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = core_count value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = pop_count value = 0 }
		all_core = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
			}
			THIS = { change_variable = { which = core_count value = 1 } }
		}
		all_core = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				THIS = { change_variable = { which = pop_count value = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
    option = {
        name = "Very Well"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 2.99 } }
				THIS = { OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 20 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 150 } } } }
			}
			country_event = 777770490
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				OR = { AND = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 2.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 5.99 } } }
				THIS = { AND = { NOT = { OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 20 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 150 } } } OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 15 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 100 } } } } }
			}
			country_event = 777770493
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				tag = FROM
				check_variable = { which = dismantlement_dollars value = 5.99 }
				THIS = { NOT = { OR = { check_variable = { which = core_count value = 15 } check_variable = { which = pop_count value = 100 } } } }
			}
			country_event = 777770496
		}
	}
}

        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall exist (Overwrite new states)"

		}
		create_alliance = FROM
    }
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall exist"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_NonOverwrite value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770500
		}
		create_alliance = FROM
    }
    option = {
        name = "Other Victors can say on $FROMCOUNTRY$"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_Apathy value = 1 }

		}
    }

        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall stay as it is"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_NonFreedom value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770500
		}
    }
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall be our vassal B[-3]!"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_OurVassal value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770500
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = dismantlement_dollars
			value = -3
		}
		set_country_flag = dismantlement_dollars_target
		CLN = { country_event = 777771700 }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 777770520
    title = "What is our stance on $FROMCOUNTRY$?"
    desc = "The Conference Chair wishes to create a $FROMCOUNTRY$. The proposal overwrites current plans, How do we respond?"
	picture = "dismantle 7"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "We agree, $FROMCOUNTRY$ Should exist!"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
			}
			relation = {
				who = THIS
				value = 20
			}
		}
		badboy = 0.1
		create_alliance = FROM
		any_country = {
			limit = {

			}
			set_variable = { which = Eighth_Victor_Complete value = 1 }

		}

country_event = {
    id = 777770550
    title = "Released from Dismantlement!"
    desc = "We have been released by the recent dismantlement!"
	picture = "dismantle 3"
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "Yes!"
        any_country = {
            limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
					check_variable = { which = Rewritable_State value = 0.99 }
				}
                exists = yes
                FROM = { exists = no civilized = yes }
				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_Overwrite value = 0.99 } }
            }
            release = FROM
			FROM = { civilized = yes }
        }
		any_country = {
            limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
					check_variable = { which = Rewritable_State value = 0.99 }
				}
                exists = yes
                FROM = { exists = no civilized = no }
				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_Overwrite value = 0.99 } }
            }
            release = FROM
			FROM = { civilized = no }
        }
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
					check_variable = { which = Rewritable_State value = 0.99 }			
				}
				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_Overwrite value = 0.99 } }
			}
            any_owned = { limit = { is_core = FROM } secede_province = THIS add_core = UTI }
        }
        any_country = {
            limit = {
				check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
                exists = yes
                FROM = { exists = no civilized = yes }
				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_NonOverwrite value = 0.99 } }
            }
            release = FROM
			FROM = { civilized = yes }
        }
		any_country = {
            limit = {
				check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
                exists = yes
                FROM = { exists = no civilized = no }
				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_NonOverwrite value = 0.99 } }
            }
            release = FROM
			FROM = { civilized = no }
        }
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }	
				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_NonOverwrite value = 0.99 } }
			}
            any_owned = { limit = { is_core = FROM } secede_province = THIS add_core = UTI }
        }
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
					check_variable = { which = Rewritable_State value = 0.99 }
				}
				OR = {
					FROM = { check_variable = { which = Existing_Chomp value = 0.99 } }
					FROM = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_OurFreedom value = 0.99 } }
				}
			}
			any_owned = { limit = { is_core = FROM } secede_province = THIS add_core = UTI }
			THIS = { set_country_flag = dont_be_weird_about_this }
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = dont_be_weird_about_this } }
			owner = {
				any_owned = { limit = { is_core = UTI is_core = THIS } remove_core = THIS add_core = CLN }
				release = UTI
				UTI = { annex_to = UTI any_owned = { limit = { is_core = CLN } add_core = THIS remove_core = CLN } all_core = { remove_core = UTI } }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				THIS = { has_country_flag = dont_be_weird_about_this }
				check_variable = { which = Secondary_Claim value = 0.99 }
			}
			THIS = { clr_country_flag = dont_be_weird_about_this }
			inherit = UTI
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				THIS = { has_country_flag = dont_be_weird_about_this }
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
			}
			THIS = { clr_country_flag = dont_be_weird_about_this }
			inherit = UTI
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { FROM = { civilized = yes } } }
			owner = {
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						is_core = UTI
					}
					secede_province = FROM
					remove_core = UTI
				}
				FROM = { civilized = yes }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = { owner = { FROM = { civilized = no } } }
			owner = {
				any_owned = {
					limit = {
						is_core = UTI
					}
					secede_province = FROM
					remove_core = UTI
				}
				FROM = { civilized = no }
			}
		}
		FROM = { set_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 0 } }
    }
}

			}

country_event = {
    id = 777771100
    title = "We may have our cores returned from $FROMCOUNTRY$ by the current dismantlement!"
    desc = "Our $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ cores are being considered."
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { which = core_count value = 0 }
		set_variable = { which = pop_count value = 0 }
		all_core = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
			}
			THIS = { change_variable = { which = core_count value = 1 } }
		}
		all_core = {
			limit = { 
				owner = { 
					check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				}
			}

		}

country_event = {

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}

			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }

			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }

    }

			modifier = { factor = 3 relation = { who = FROM value = 160 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 140 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			 
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }

    }

country_event = {
    id = 777772000
    title = "What would you like to do with $FROMCOUNTRY$?"
    desc = "The concept of $FROMCOUNTRY$ is present within the borders of the defeated, should we demand the creation of a $FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ state?"
	picture = "dismantle 8"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				have_core_in = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_recently_lost_war = yes
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }
	
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall exist (Overwrite new states)"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_Overwrite value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770430
		}
		create_alliance = FROM
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 5 government = democracy }
			modifier = { factor = 5 relation = { who = FROM value = 199 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 relation = { who = FROM value = 180 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 relation = { who = FROM value = 160 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 140 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			 
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall exist"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_NonOverwrite value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770430	
		}
		create_alliance = FROM
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 4
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 4 government = democracy }

			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {

		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_NonFreedom value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 0 }

			modifier = { factor = 5 has_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 15 badboy = 23 }

			country_event = 777770430

		change_variable = {
			which = dismantlement_dollars
			value = -6
		}
		set_country_flag = dismantlement_dollars_target
		CLN = { country_event = 777771700 }
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 1

country_event = {
    id = 777772300
    title = "What should be done with the $FROMCOUNTRY$ puppet state?"
    desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ is a puppet regime, should we reorganize their government?"
	picture = "dismantle 21"
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				OR = { AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = democracy government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism government = hms_government government = constitutional_empire } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship government = parliamentary_republic government = prussian_constitutionalism } } THIS = { OR = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } THIS = { OR = { government = presidential_dictatorship government = fascist_dictatorship } } } AND = { FROM = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } THIS = { OR = { government = absolute_monarchy government = absolute_empire government = semi_constitutional_empire } } } }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = conflicting_government_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				badboy = 0.8
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = infamous_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				have_core_in = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				OR = {
					has_recently_lost_war = yes
					is_disarmed = yes
					military_access = THIS
				}
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				FROM = { slavery = yes_slavery }
				THIS = { slavery = yes_slavery }
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = FROM
				truce_with = THIS
			}
			THIS = { set_country_flag = truce_with_this_penalty }
		}
		set_country_flag = annex_overwrite
    }
	
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall be independent!"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Puppet_Freedom value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770431
		}
		create_alliance = FROM
        ai_chance = {
            factor = 5
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_flag = common_government_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 5 government = democracy }
			modifier = { factor = 5 relation = { who = FROM value = 199 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 relation = { who = FROM value = 180 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 relation = { who = FROM value = 160 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 140 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 relation = { who = FROM value = 120 } }
			 
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = holdout_slavery_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_country_flag = recent_state_bonus }
			modifier = { factor = 0.5 has_country_flag = we_control_core_penalty }
			modifier = { factor = 0.05 badboy = 23 }
			modifier = { factor = 0.75 badboy = 17 }
        }
    }
    option = {
